2019-01-23 08:34:21,661 [31] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@BinData
SELECT T.BIN_NO
              ,T.CREATION_DATE
              ,CASE T2.BIN_STATUS WHEN CHAR(36) THEN '正常' ELSE '异常' END BIN_STATUS
              ,CASE T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN '_' THEN '在库' WHEN 'O' THEN '预约出库' WHEN 'I' THEN '预约入库' WHEN 'M' THEN '移库' ELSE '其他' END BIN_BIZ_STATUS
              ,T.PALLET_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NAME
              ,T1.PRODUCT_GUID
              ,T1.PRODUCT_DATE
              ,T1.PRODUCT_QTY
              ,T1.MAIN_UNIT
         FROM WBS_BIN T
         LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
         LEFT JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2 ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
       where   T.CREATION_DATE >= @param0    AND  T.CREATION_DATE <= 1+ @param1
参数：
@param0=2018/1/22 0:00:00
@param1=2019/1/23 0:00:00

2019-01-23 08:34:48,994 [29] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-23 08:34:51,125 [29] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC

2019-01-23 08:35:59,322 [29] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@BinData
SELECT T.BIN_NO
              ,T.CREATION_DATE
              ,CASE T2.BIN_STATUS WHEN CHAR(36) THEN '正常' ELSE '异常' END BIN_STATUS
              ,CASE T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN '_' THEN '在库' WHEN 'O' THEN '预约出库' WHEN 'I' THEN '预约入库' WHEN 'M' THEN '移库' ELSE '其他' END BIN_BIZ_STATUS
              ,T.PALLET_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NAME
              ,T1.PRODUCT_GUID
              ,T1.PRODUCT_DATE
              ,T1.PRODUCT_QTY
              ,T1.MAIN_UNIT
         FROM WBS_BIN T
         LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
         LEFT JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2 ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
       where   T.CREATION_DATE >= @param0    AND  T.CREATION_DATE <= 1+ @param1

2019-01-23 08:36:04,263 [57] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@InOutBinHistory
SELECT T.BIN_GUID,
        T.BIN_NO,
        CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库'
             WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库'
        END IO_TYPE,
        T.CREATION_DATE,
        T.PALLET_NO,
        ISNULL(T1.MATER_NO,T2.MATER_NO) MATER_NO,
        ISNULL(T1.MATER_NAME,T2.MATER_NAME) MATER_NAME,
        CASE WHEN T.FINISH_FLAG IS NULL OR T.FINISH_FLAG = '_' THEN '正常'
        ELSE T.FINISH_FLAG END FINISH_FLAG,
        CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN ISNULL(T3.SLOC_NO,T4.SLOC_NO)
             WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN ISNULL(T3.ELOC_NO,T4.ELOC_NO) 
        END LOC_NO,
        ISNULL(T3.TASK_NO,T4.TASK_NO) TASK_NO,
        ISNULL(T3.CREATION_DATE,T4.CREATION_DATE) CREATE_TASK_DATE,
        ISNULL(T3.TASK_EXEC_START_DT,T4.TASK_EXEC_START_DT) TASK_EXEC_START_DT,
        ISNULL(T3.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,T4.TASK_EXEC_END_DT) TASK_EXEC_END_DT
        FROM Z50_WBS_BIN T
        LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
        LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T2 ON T2.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
        LEFT JOIN WBS_TASK T3 ON T3.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
        LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_TASK T4 ON T4.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
       where   T.CREATION_DATE >= @param0    AND  T.CREATION_DATE <= 1+ @param1
参数：
@param0=2019/1/18 0:00:00
@param1=2019/1/23 0:00:00

2019-01-23 08:46:55,703 [49] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：
